    <script>
     window.GCI = window.GCI || {
      modules: {}      
};
function callCenterPencil () {
    var currentNode = document.querySelector("#pencil");
    var jsNumberSync = GCI.digitalData.pageData.customerService;
    var newNode = document.createElement("span");
    // newNode.id = "sitewidePencil";
    newNode.innerHTML =
        '&nbsp; <a href="tel:1' +
        jsNumberSync +
        ' class="cta-link">' +
        jsNumberSync +
    "</a>";
    currentNode.parentNode.replaceChild(newNode, currentNode);
}   
if (GCI.externalResourcesLoaded) {
    callCenterPencil();
    } else {
    document.addEventListener(
        'externalResourcesLoaded',
        callCenterPencil,
        false
    );
}
    </script>
